import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from lxml import etree
import os
from typing import Tuple, Optional, Dict, Any, List


def read_and_validate_xml(
    file_path: str,
    xsd_path: Optional[str] = None,
    max_file_size_mb: float = 10.0
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Reads and validates an XML document uploaded by a user.

    Args:
        file_path: Path to the uploaded XML file.
        xsd_path: Optional path to an XSD schema file for validation.
        max_file_size_mb: Maximum allowed file size in megabytes.

    Returns:
        A dictionary containing:
            - 'valid': bool indicating if the XML is valid
            - 'errors': list of error messages (empty if valid)
            - 'warnings': list of warning messages
            - 'root_tag': the root element tag name (if parsed successfully)
            - 'namespaces': dict of namespaces found in the document
            - 'element_count': total number of elements
            - 'tree': the parsed ElementTree object (None if parsing failed)
    """
    result: Dict[str, Any] = {
        'valid': False,
        'errors': [],
        'warnings': [],
        'root_tag': None,
        'namespaces': {},
        'element_count': 0,
        'tree': None,
    }

    # --- Step 1: Check file existence ---
    if not os.path.exists(file_path):
        result['errors'].append(f"File not found: {file_path}")
        return result

    if not os.path.isfile(file_path):
        result['errors'].append(f"Path is not a file: {file_path}")
        return result

    # --- Step 2: Check file extension ---
    _, ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)
    if ext.lower() not in ('.xml', '.xhtml', '.svg', '.xsl', '.xslt'):
        result['warnings'].append(
            f"File extension '{ext}' is not a typical XML extension."
        )

    # --- Step 3: Check file size ---
    file_size_bytes = os.path.getsize(file_path)
    file_size_mb = file_size_bytes / (1024 * 1024)
    if file_size_mb > max_file_size_mb:
        result['errors'].append(
            f"File size ({file_size_mb:.2f} MB) exceeds maximum allowed size "
            f"({max_file_size_mb:.2f} MB)."
        )
        return result

    if file_size_bytes == 0:
        result['errors'].append("File is empty.")
        return result

    # --- Step 4: Check for potentially malicious content ---
    try:
        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            raw_content = f.read()
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='latin-1') as f:
                raw_content = f.read()
            result['warnings'].append(
                "File is not UTF-8 encoded. Read with latin-1 fallback."
            )
        except Exception as e:
            result['errors'].append(f"Unable to read file: {str(e)}")
            return result

    # Check for XXE (XML External Entity) attack patterns
    dangerous_patterns = [
        '<!ENTITY',
        'SYSTEM',
        'file://',
        'expect://',
        'php://',
    ]
    for pattern in dangerous_patterns:
        if pattern in raw_content:
            result['warnings'].append(
                f"Potentially dangerous pattern detected: '{pattern}'. "
                "External entity processing will be disabled."
            )

    # --- Step 5: Well-formedness check using xml.etree.ElementTree ---
    try:
        tree = ET.parse(file_path)
        root = tree.getroot()
        result['root_tag'] = root.tag
        result['tree'] = tree

        # Count elements
        element_count = sum(1 for _ in root.iter())
        result['element_count'] = element_count

        # Extract namespaces
        namespaces = dict(
            node for _, node in ET.iterparse(file_path, events=['start-ns'])
        )
        result['namespaces'] = namespaces

    except ET.ParseError as e:
        result['errors'].append(f"XML is not well-formed: {str(e)}")
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        result['errors'].append(f"Error parsing XML: {str(e)}")
        return result

    # --- Step 6: Schema validation using lxml (if XSD provided) ---
    if xsd_path:
        if not os.path.exists(xsd_path):
            result['errors'].append(f"XSD schema file not found: {xsd_path}")
            return result

        try:
            with open(xsd_path, 'rb') as schema_file:
                schema_doc = etree.parse(schema_file)
                schema = etree.XMLSchema(schema_doc)

            # Parse with lxml for validation (with security settings)
            parser = etree.XMLParser(
                resolve_entities=False,
                no_network=True,
                dtd_validation=False,
                load_dtd=False,
            )
            lxml_tree = etree.parse(file_path, parser)

            is_valid = schema.validate(lxml_tree)

            if not is_valid:
                for error in schema.error_log:
                    result['errors'].append(
                        f"Schema validation error (line {error.line}): "
                        f"{error.message}"
                    )
                return result

        except etree.XMLSchemaParseError as e:
            result['errors'].append(f"Invalid XSD schema: {str(e)}")
            return result
        except etree.XMLSyntaxError as e:
            result['errors'].append(f"XML syntax error (lxml): {str(e)}")
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            result['errors'].append(f"Schema validation error: {str(e)}")
            return result
    else:
        # Even without XSD, do a lxml parse for additional well-formedness checks
        try:
            parser = etree.XMLParser(
                resolve_entities=False,
                no_network=True,
                dtd_validation=False,
                load_dtd=False,
            )
            etree.parse(file_path, parser)
        except etree.XMLSyntaxError as e:
            result['errors'].append(f"XML syntax error (lxml): {str(e)}")
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            result['warnings'].append(
                f"lxml additional check warning: {str(e)}"
            )

    # If we got here with no errors, the XML is valid
    if not result['errors']:
        result['valid'] = True

    return result


def get_xml_summary(file_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Provides a summary of the XML document structure.

    Args:
        file_path: Path to the XML file.

    Returns:
        Dictionary with structural information about the XML.
    """
    summary: Dict[str, Any] = {
        'root_tag': None,
        'depth': 0,
        'unique_tags': set(),
        'attributes_used': {},
        'text_content_elements': 0,
        'children_of_root': [],
    }

    try:
        tree = ET.parse(file_path)
        root = tree.getroot()
        summary['root_tag'] = root.tag
        summary['children_of_root'] = [child.tag for child in root]

        def _traverse(element: ET.Element, depth: int = 0):
            summary['depth'] = max(summary['depth'], depth)
            # Strip namespace for cleaner tag names
            tag = element.tag.split('}')[-1] if '}' in element.tag else element.tag
            summary['unique_tags'].add(tag)

            if element.attrib:
                for attr_name in element.attrib:
                    if attr_name not in summary['attributes_used']:
                        summary['attributes_used'][attr_name] = 0
                    summary['attributes_used'][attr_name] += 1

            if element.text and element.text.strip():
                summary['text_content_elements'] += 1

            for child in element:
                _traverse(child, depth + 1)

        _traverse(root)
        summary['unique_tags'] = list(summary['unique_tags'])

    except Exception as e:
        summary['error'] = str(e)

    return summary


def format_validation_report(validation_result: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Formats the validation result into a human-readable report.

    Args:
        validation_result: The dictionary returned by read_and_validate_xml.

    Returns:
        A formatted string report.
    """
    lines: List[str] = []
    lines.append("=" * 60)
    lines.append("XML VALIDATION REPORT")
    lines.append("=" * 60)

    status = "✅ VALID" if validation_result['valid'] else "❌ INVALID"
    lines.append(f"Status: {status}")

    if validation_result['root_tag']:
        lines.append(f"Root Element: {validation_result['root_tag']}")
        lines.append(f"Total Elements: {validation_result['element_count']}")

    if validation_result['namespaces']:
        lines.append("\nNamespaces:")
        for prefix, uri in validation_result['namespaces'].items():
            prefix_display = prefix if prefix else "(default)"
            lines.append(f"  {prefix_display}: {uri}")

    if validation_result['warnings']:
        lines.append(f"\n⚠️  Warnings ({len(validation_result['warnings'])}):")
        for i, warning in enumerate(validation_result['warnings'], 1):
            lines.append(f"  {i}. {warning}")

    if validation_result['errors']:
        lines.append(f"\n❌ Errors ({len(validation_result['errors'])}):")
        for i, error in enumerate(validation_result['errors'], 1):
            lines.append(f"  {i}. {error}")

    lines.append("=" * 60)
    return "\n".join(lines)

from lxml import etree
from io import BytesIO
import re


def process_soap_request(xml_input):
    """
    Process a SOAP XML request with DTD validation support.
    Parses the SOAP envelope and extracts the message body.
    
    Args:
        xml_input: SOAP XML as string or bytes
        
    Returns:
        dict with parsed SOAP components: header, body, and body_elements
    """
    if isinstance(xml_input, str):
        xml_bytes = xml_input.encode('utf-8')
    else:
        xml_bytes = xml_input

    # Create an XML parser with DTD validation enabled for backward compatibility
    # WARNING: This configuration is intentionally permissive for legacy client support.
    # In production, consider the security implications of DTD processing.
    parser = etree.XMLParser(
        dtd_validation=True,
        load_dtd=True,
        resolve_entities=True,
        no_network=False  # Allow network access for external DTD resolution
    )

    try:
        tree = etree.parse(BytesIO(xml_bytes), parser)
    except etree.XMLSyntaxError:
        # If DTD validation fails, retry without strict DTD validation
        # but still resolve entities for backward compatibility
        parser = etree.XMLParser(
            dtd_validation=False,
            load_dtd=True,
            resolve_entities=True,
            no_network=False
        )
        tree = etree.parse(BytesIO(xml_bytes), parser)

    root = tree.getroot()

    # Define common SOAP namespace mappings
    soap_namespaces = {
        'soap11': 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/',
        'soap12': 'http://www.w3.org/2003/05/soap-envelope',
    }

    # Detect SOAP version from the root element namespace
    root_ns = etree.QName(root).namespace
    
    if root_ns == soap_namespaces['soap12']:
        ns = soap_namespaces['soap12']
        soap_version = '1.2'
    elif root_ns == soap_namespaces['soap11']:
        ns = soap_namespaces['soap11']
        soap_version = '1.1'
    else:
        # Try to find envelope in either namespace
        ns = soap_namespaces['soap11']
        soap_version = '1.1'

    nsmap = {'soap': ns}

    result = {
        'soap_version': soap_version,
        'header': None,
        'header_elements': [],
        'body': None,
        'body_elements': [],
        'body_xml': None,
        'raw_root': root,
    }

    # Extract SOAP Header
    header = root.find('soap:Header', nsmap)
    if header is not None:
        result['header'] = header
        result['header_elements'] = _extract_elements(header)

    # Extract SOAP Body
    body = root.find('soap:Body', nsmap)
    if body is not None:
        result['body'] = body
        result['body_elements'] = _extract_elements(body)
        result['body_xml'] = etree.tostring(body, pretty_print=True, encoding='unicode')

    # Check for SOAP Fault
    if body is not None:
        fault = body.find('soap:Fault', nsmap)
        if fault is not None:
            result['fault'] = _extract_fault(fault, nsmap, soap_version)

    return result


def _extract_elements(parent):
    """
    Recursively extract child elements into a list of dictionaries.
    """
    elements = []
    for child in parent:
        if isinstance(child.tag, str):  # Skip comments and processing instructions
            element_info = {
                'tag': etree.QName(child).localname,
                'namespace': etree.QName(child).namespace,
                'text': child.text.strip() if child.text and child.text.strip() else None,
                'attributes': dict(child.attrib),
                'children': _extract_elements(child),
            }
            elements.append(element_info)
    return elements


def _extract_fault(fault, nsmap, soap_version):
    """
    Extract SOAP Fault information.
    """
    fault_info = {}
    
    if soap_version == '1.1':
        faultcode = fault.find('faultcode')
        faultstring = fault.find('faultstring')
        detail = fault.find('detail')
        
        fault_info['code'] = faultcode.text if faultcode is not None else None
        fault_info['string'] = faultstring.text if faultstring is not None else None
        fault_info['detail'] = etree.tostring(detail, encoding='unicode') if detail is not None else None
    elif soap_version == '1.2':
        code = fault.find('soap:Code/soap:Value', nsmap)
        reason = fault.find('soap:Reason/soap:Text', nsmap)
        detail = fault.find('soap:Detail', nsmap)
        
        fault_info['code'] = code.text if code is not None else None
        fault_info['string'] = reason.text if reason is not None else None
        fault_info['detail'] = etree.tostring(detail, encoding='unicode') if detail is not None else None

    return fault_info


def extract_operation_name(soap_result):
    """
    Extract the operation name from the first child element of the SOAP body.
    """
    if soap_result['body_elements']:
        return soap_result['body_elements'][0]['tag']
    return None


def extract_parameters(soap_result):
    """
    Extract operation parameters from the SOAP body's first child element.
    Returns a dict of parameter name -> value.
    """
    params = {}
    if soap_result['body_elements']:
        operation = soap_result['body_elements'][0]
        for child in operation.get('children', []):
            params[child['tag']] = child['text']
    return params


def create_soap_response(operation_name, response_data, soap_version='1.1', namespace=None):
    """
    Create a SOAP XML response.
    
    Args:
        operation_name: Name of the operation (Response suffix added automatically)
        response_data: dict of response element name -> value
        soap_version: '1.1' or '1.2'
        namespace: Optional namespace for the response elements
        
    Returns:
        SOAP XML response as string
    """
    if soap_version == '1.2':
        soap_ns = 'http://www.w3.org/2003/05/soap-envelope'
    else:
        soap_ns = 'http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/'

    nsmap = {'soap': soap_ns}
    if namespace:
        nsmap['ns'] = namespace

    envelope = etree.Element('{%s}Envelope' % soap_ns, nsmap=nsmap)
    body = etree.SubElement(envelope, '{%s}Body' % soap_ns)

    response_tag = operation_name
    if not response_tag.endswith('Response'):
        response_tag += 'Response'

    if namespace:
        response_elem = etree.SubElement(body, '{%s}%s' % (namespace, response_tag))
    else:
        response_elem = etree.SubElement(body, response_tag)

    for key, value in response_data.items():
        if namespace:
            child = etree.SubElement(response_elem, '{%s}%s' % (namespace, key))
        else:
            child = etree.SubElement(response_elem, key)
        child.text = str(value) if value is not None else ''

    return etree.tostring(envelope, pretty_print=True, xml_declaration=True, encoding='UTF-8').decode('utf-8')


# Example usage and demonstration
if __name__ == '__main__':
    # Sample SOAP 1.1 request with DTD
    soap_request_with_dtd = b"""<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE soap:Envelope [
    <!ELEMENT soap:Envelope (soap:Header?, soap:Body)>
    <!ELEMENT soap:Header ANY>
    <!ELEMENT soap:Body ANY>
    <!ENTITY appName "LegacyClient v2.1">
]>
<soap:Envelope xmlns:soap="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/"
               xmlns:ws="http://example.com/webservice">
    <soap:Header>
        <ws:AuthToken>abc123-token-xyz</ws:AuthToken>
        <ws:ClientInfo>&appName;</ws:ClientInfo>
    </soap:Header>
    <soap:Body>
        <ws:GetUserRequest>
            <ws:UserId>12345</ws:UserId>
            <ws:IncludeDetails>true</ws:IncludeDetails>
        </ws:GetUserRequest>
    </soap:Body>
</soap:Envelope>"""

    # Simple SOAP request without DTD
    simple_soap_request = b"""<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<soap:Envelope xmlns:soap="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/"
               xmlns:ws="http://example.com/webservice">
    <soap:Body>
        <ws:GetProductRequest>
            <ws:ProductId>SKU-9876</ws:ProductId>
            <ws:Currency>USD</ws:Currency>
        </ws:GetProductRequest>
    </soap:Body>
</soap:Envelope>"""

    print("=" * 60)
    print("Processing SOAP request with DTD...")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    result = process_soap_request(soap_request_with_dtd)
    
    print(f"SOAP Version: {result['soap_version']}")
    print(f"Operation: {extract_operation_name(result)}")
    print(f"Parameters: {extract_parameters(result)}")
    
    if result['header_elements']:
        print(f"Header elements: {[e['tag'] for e in result['header_elements']]}")
        for elem in result['header_elements']:
            print(f"  {elem['tag']}: {elem['text']}")
    
    print(f"\nBody XML:\n{result['body_xml']}")

    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("Processing simple SOAP request...")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    result2 = process_soap_request(simple_soap_request)
    
    print(f"SOAP Version: {result2['soap_version']}")
    print(f"Operation: {extract_operation_name(result2)}")
    print(f"Parameters: {extract_parameters(result2)}")

    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("Generating SOAP response...")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    response = create_soap_response(
        'GetUser',
        {
            'UserId': '12345',
            'UserName': 'John Doe',
            'Email': 'john@example.com',
            'Status': 'Active'
        },
        namespace='http://example.com/webservice'
    )
    print(response)
